	<p>
	<b>Dear Readers, <br>
	We highly recommend registering yourselves as members on the website. We host Tamil novels that are categorized under Family Romance and we hope that only the readers who are of eligible age read the stories of this genre. The website is age compliant as well.</b></p>
<p>
	<b>We hereby claim that we do not present adult or violent or offensive content, explicit or otherwise and the understanding of it completely depends on the reader's discretion. We don’t intend to offend the readers’ sentiments in any way.</b></p>
<p>
	<b>All the works here are intellectual property of the writers and are strictly copyrighted to the respective writers. Reproducing the same in any format, without writer’s permission, is subject to legal actions. </b></p>
